like all medicines , this medicine can cause side effects , although not everybody gets them . some side effects can be serious . tell your doctor straight away if you notice any of the following : very common ( may affect more than 1 in 10 people ) difficulty breathing or swallowing , swelling of the face , lips , tongue , or throat , skin rash , itching and hives ( signs of allergic reaction ). other side effects may include : very common ( may affect more than 1 in 10 people ) sore throat , runny nose , difficulty in breathing or shortness of breath , wheezing or coughing . common ( may affect up to 1 in 10 people ) fungal infections of the mouth , mouth or throat and may be signs of a urinary tract infection ( e . g . thrush and / or mucosal mucosal infection ). signs of urinary tract infection such as headache , fast heart beat , cough , fast heart beat , cough , stuffy nose , hoarseness , diarrhoea , abdominal pain , nausea , vomiting , abdominal pain , nausea , vomiting , abdominal pain , nausea , vomiting , abdominal pain , nausea and / or vomiting ( may be signs of a urinary tract infection ) bone pain , muscle pain , fever , muscle pain , bone pain , pain in extremity . uncommon ( may affect up to 1 in 100 people ) high level of sugar in the blood , candidiasis , dry mouth , skin rash , difficulty in breathing or swallowing , swelling of the face , lips , tongue or throat ( signs of cataract ) reporting of side effects if you get any side effects , talk to your doctor or pharmacist . this includes any possible side effects not listed in this leaflet . you can also report side effects directly via the national reporting system listed in appendix v . by reporting side effects you can help provide more information on the safety of this medicine .
like all medicines , clopidogrel_acino_pharma_gmbh can cause side effects , although not everybody gets them . common side effects ( may affect up to 1 in 10 people ): headache , stomach ulcer , vomiting , nausea , constipation , excessive gas in stomach or intestines , rashes , itching , dizziness , sensation of tingling and numbness . rare side effect ( may affect up to 1 in 1 , 000 people ): vertigo . very rare side effects ( may affect up to 1 in 10 , 000 people ): jaundice ; severe abdominal pain with or without back pain ; fever , breathing difficulties sometimes associated with cough ; generalised allergic reactions ( for example , overall sensation of heat with sudden general discomfort until cough ); swelling in the mouth ; blisters of the skin ; confusion ; hallucinations ; joint pain ; muscular pain ; changes in the way things taste . in addition , your doctor may identify changes in your blood or urine test results . if any of the side effects gets serious , or if you notice any side effects not listed in this leaflet , please tell your doctor or pharmacist .
